fcg"><a class="_5pcq" href="/Queen/posts/10152716058562362"><abbr title="Monday, February 2, 2015 at 7:04am" data-utime="1422889495" data-shorten="1" class="_5ptz">February 2 at 7:04am</abbr></a></span></span> Â· <a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Public" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator _5pcq" href="#" role="button"><i class="lock img sp_j2SLQ6WAPvh sx_e8f385"></i></a></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><div id="id_54d946e317b988407963180" class="text_exposed_root"><p>Roger Taylor&#039;s solo albums &quot;Fun in Space&quot; and &quot;Strange Frontier&quot; have been expanded for reissue on March 24th in both CD and vinyl formats. </p><p> The Fun in Space LP will be reissued on vinyl for the time since its 1981 release. The first run will be on clear vinyl (with black vinyl to follow) and contains a reproduction of the original album&#039;s full color inner sleeve with lyrics. The CD version, housed in a digipak, contains three bonus tracks: both sides of Taylor&#039;s 1977 solo of<span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">fering (&quot;I Wanna Testify&quot; b/w &quot;Turn on the TV&quot;) and the U.K. single version of the album&#039;s &quot;My Country I &amp; II&quot; (issued as &quot;My Country&quot;).</span></p><div class="text_exposed_show"><p> Strange Frontier will be reissued on translucent red vinyl for the first pressing (black vinyl for future runs) with all original packaging elements replicated. The CD, contained in a digipak, features five bonus tracks: remixes of the album&#039;s singles &quot;Man on Fire,&quot; &quot;I Cry for You (Love, Hope and Confusion)&quot; and &quot;Strange Frontier.&quot; It also contains the B-side to the title cut, &quot;Two Sharp Pencils (Get Bad).&quot;</p><p> With this material currently only available in the 10 CD/1 DVD collection The Lot, this is the first time versions of the individual albums will be offered outside of that package.</p><p> Fun in Space:<br /> No Violins <br /> Laugh or Cry <br /> Future Management <br /> My Country I &amp; II <br /> Good Times Are Now <br /> Magic Is Loose <br /> Interlude in Constantinople <br /> Airheads <br /> Fun in Space </p><p> CD Bonus Tracks: <br /> I Wanna Testify <br /> Turn on the TV <br /> My Country (Single Version)</p><p> Strange Frontier:<br /> Strange Frontier <br /> Beautiful Dreams <br /> Man on Fire <br /> Racing in the Street <br /> Masters of War <br /> Killing Time <br /> Abandonfire <br /> Young Love <br /> It&#039;s an Illusion <br /> I Cry for You </p><p> CD bonus Tracks: <br /> Man on Fire (Extended Version) <br /> I Cry for You (Single Remix) <br /> Strange Frontier (Extended Remix) <br /> I Cry for You (Extended Remix) <br /> Two Sharp Pencils (Get Bad) </p><p> More details to follow!</p><p> <a
